const inp = (extra = {}) => ({ background: “rgba(255,255,255,0.06)”, border: “1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.12)”, borderRadius: 10, color: “white”, padding: “11px 14px”, fontSize: 14, width: “100%”, boxSizing: “border-box”, outline: “none”, fontFamily: “inherit”, transition: “border-color 0.2s”, …extra, }); function Badge({ text }) { const palette = { “Muscle Gain”: [”#f97316”,”#431407”], “Weight Loss”: [”#06b6d4”,”#0a2535”], “Endurance”: [”#10b981”,”#052e1c”], “Flexibility”: [”#8b5cf6”,”#2e1065”], “Athletic Performance”: [”#f59e0b”,”#341a00”], “General Fitness”: [”#6366f1”,”#1e1b4b”], Beginner: [”#10b981”,”#052e1c”], Intermediate: [”#f59e0b”,”#341a00”], Advanced: [”#ef4444”,”#3b0000”], }; const [fg, bg] = palette[text] || [”#94a3b8”, “#1e293b”]; return {text}; } function hexToRgb(hex) { const r = parseInt(hex.slice(1,3),16), g = parseInt(hex.slice(3,5),16), b = parseInt(hex.slice(5,7),16); return `${r},${g},${b}`; } // ─── LOGIN ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── function LoginScreen({ onLogin }) { const [mode, setMode] = useState(“client”); const [email, setEmail] = useState(””); const [password, setPassword] = useState(””); const [error, setError] = useState(””); const [show, setShow] = useState(false); const [loggingIn, setLoggingIn] = useState(false); const handleLogin = async ()
